That morning we caught a Violet-headed Hummingbird, Rufous-cheeked Hummingbird and Olive-striped Flycatcher with the same reaction from the others in our group as in the previous day. I have banded over 25,000 birds in my life and I never cease to marvel at what birds look like in the hand.  While handling the birds I missed the Tooth-billed Hummingbird the rest of our group saw at camp and that turned out to be the last opportunity I would have to see this specialty of the Cerro Pirre. By 9:00 we were headed back down the trail to Cana and birding was very productive. We arrived at Cana about 13:00 and after lunch birded around the compound, winding up the day around the airstrip while looking at several species of Macaws. URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS94340125	11590.31	species	Great Green Macaw	Ara ambiguus			3			Panama	PA	Darién	PA-5				Darien--Cerro Pirre Trail	L934379	H	7.8610011	-77.6678467	1999-02-17	07:30:00	Coverage: The prolonged, and at times driving rain through the night added to our level of anxiety about hiking to the top of Cerro Pirre in the morning.  We arose at 6:00 about the same time it stopped raining.  After breakfast we were on the trial by 7:30.  We all thought it a bit odd that Carmen Martino would tell us all to take a walking stick but as we would soon discover it was the only way we would be able to keep our balance on the very slick muddy trail up the mountain. We stopped many times to bird the many flocks we encountered on the hike. At 13:00 it started raining again making conditions on the trail even worse. For some inexplicable reason I had sent my rain gear up with the pack animals and without it I got soaked. As it turned out everyone else with rain gear got just as wet as I did from the humidity and sweat trapped under their rain gear.  We arrived at camp at about 13:30 and after a quick lunch that awaited us we started birding up the ridge. Despite the continuing rain we found many good-sized flocks and the birding was excellent.  We birded until dark and returned to camp for dinner and a welcomed nights sleep in individual tents where it was relatively dry.  There was just no getting around the humidity that we would experience during our entire stay in the Darien----Other observers: Brian Daniels, Dave De Sante, Pete Ginsberg, Dean Vanier, Tom Wurster		obs27049	Peter	Ginsburg	S6567283	eBird - Traveling  Count	EBIRD	480	10		6	1	G177320	1	0		
URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS94340285	11590.31	species	Great Green Macaw	Ara ambiguus			10			Panama	PA	Darién	PA-5				Darien--Boca de Cupe Trail	L934325	H	7.8419553	-77.6101685	1999-02-16	06:30:00	Coverage: We left camp at about 6:30 and spent the morning birding Boca de Cupe trail where we found a small antswarm.  At noon we returned to camp for lunch and again birded the grounds.  The large fruiting trees above camp and smaller shrubs around the grounds provided ample fruit and flowers for an assortment of guans, chachalacas, hummingbirds, tanagers and even a few cotingas.  In the afternoon we took the trail down the Rio Seteganti and as in the morning, found an antswarm, which was very productive. Unfortunately by 16:00 it began to rain and by the time we returned to camp it was raining very hard. Late in the afternoon it finally stopped raining and we were able to bird the airstrip for about a half-hour before dinner. I was very pleased at the quality of our meals at Cana and given the difficulty and lack of good equipment in the kitchen it was amazing the food was as good as it was.  At about mid-night it started raining again and continued, sometimes with hard driving rain that awoke us several times during the night. ----Other observers: Brian Daniels, Dave De Sante, Pete Ginsberg, Dean Vanier, Tom Wurster.		obs27049	Peter	Ginsburg	S6567286	eBird - Traveling  Count	EBIRD	480	5		6	1	G177321	1	0

In the afternoon we took the trail down the Rio Seteganti and as in the morning, found an antswarm, which was very productive. Unfortunately by 16:00 it began to rain and by the time we returned to camp it was raining very hard. Late in the afternoon it finally stopped raining and we were able to bird the airstrip for about a half-hour before dinner. I was very pleased at the quality of our meals at Cana and given the difficulty and lack of good equipment in the kitchen it was amazing the food was as good as it was.  At about mid-night it started raining again and continued, sometimes with hard driving rain that awoke us several times during the night. ----Other observers: Brian Daniels, Dave De Sante, Pete Ginsburg, Dean Vanier, Tom Wurster.		obs102836	Mike	San Miguel	S6554988	eBird - Traveling  Count	EBIRD	480	5		6	1	G177321	1	0
